<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:несуразный.html>несура́зный</a> (21351)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">not</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сура́зный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">suráznyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">prominent, beautiful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">су-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">su-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">with</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(originally) stroke, cut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:несущественный.html>несуще́ственный</a> (16270)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:существенный.html>суще́ственный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">suščéstvennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***нет.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a> (59)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">нѣту</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nětu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nětu</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ne</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">not</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*e</i>, short form of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*estь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">is</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tu</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">there, here</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">net</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>no
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ješčó <b>net</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">not yet</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">net</span>) (<i>impersonal verb</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>there is no, there are no (+ <i>genitive</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>Здесь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́г</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Zdesʹ <b>net</b> doróg.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">There are no roads here.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́г</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá <b>net</b> knig.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I have no books. (literally, “There are no books with me.”)</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jevó <b>net</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He’s not here. (literally, “There is no him [here].”)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The past tense of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">net</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">né bylo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and the future tense is <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne búdet</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***нету.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>не́ту</a> (1693)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">нѣту</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nětu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">нѣтъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nětŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. From older <b>*<a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> ѥ <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>ту</a></b> (it is not here), where <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>ту</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тут.html>тут</a>, also colloquial <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">не́туть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nétutĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), was originally an ethical dative (<i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">-ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, dative <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">-ти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Often proscribed in favor of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">net</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li>In the colloquial register, usage depends largely on the speaker's personal attitude towards this word; there is a range from active users to those who oppose it unconditionally.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">net</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>ту</a></b>
</p><p>Предикатив, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:частица.html>части́ца</a>; неизменяемое.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> restless
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неугомонный.html>неугомо́нный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neugomónnyj</b> rebjónok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fidgety child</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> indefatigable, ever-active</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>го<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>мо́н<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>неугомо́ннее, неугомо́нней.</i>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неудачник.html>неуда́чник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neudáčnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неудачник.html>неуда́чника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неудачник.html>неуда́чники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неудачник.html>неуда́чников</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">неуда́чница</b>)

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
